         function computeScrollHeight() {
					var height = jQuery(window).height();
					jQuery("#tagListWrapper").css({height: height-210, overflow:"auto", "overflow-x": "hidden"});
				}
				jQuery( document ).ready(function() {
					computeScrollHeight();
					jQuery( window ).resize(function() {
						computeScrollHeight();

      <script type="text/javascript">
       function getStatsForThemeMiniStats() {
		// Call ajax request only if data is not here.
		if ($("#upv_1058404").text() == "Loading..." ) {
			jQuery.getJSON("/stats/theme/1058404?view=json", function(json){
				jQuery("#upv_1058404").empty();
				if (json.stats &amp;&amp; json.stats.uniqueVisitors &gt;= 0) {
					jQuery("#upv_1058404").append(json.stats.uniqueVisitors);				
				} else {
					jQuery("#upv_1058404").append("Not available");
				}
			});
		}
	}
      </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var themeActionsBanner = null;
	jQuery(document).ready(function() {
		themeActionsBanner = jQuery("#theme-actions-banner");
		jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
			if(parseInt(jQuery(this).scrollTop(), 10) &gt; 51) {
				themeActionsBanner.addClass("theme-actions-banner-fixed");
				jQuery("#admin-stuff").css("top", "41px");
			} else {
				themeActionsBanner.removeClass("theme-actions-banner-fixed");
				jQuery("#admin-stuff").css("top", "10px");
			}
		});
	});
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    var logoContainer;
		var infosContainer;
		var logoToHome;
		jQuery(document).ready(function() {
			logoContainer = jQuery(".headSection.head-section-logo");
			infosContainer = jQuery(".headSection.head-section-infos");

			logoToHome = jQuery("#logoToHome", logoContainer);
			//makes the logo Rumble
			logoToHome.jrumble({
				x: 0,
				y: 0,
				rotation: 4,
				speed: 75
			});
			logoToHome.hover(function() {
				var logo = $(this);
				logo.trigger('startRumble');
				// Stop 500ms after
				setTimeout(function() {
					logo.trigger('stopRumble');
				}, 500);
			}, function(){
				$(this).trigger('stopRumble');
			});
		});
   </script>

       jQuery(document).ready(function() {
        	jQuery("body").append(jQuery("#viewboxOverlay"));
        	jQuery("#allPage").prepend(jQuery("#thePostToPrintOverlay"));
            jQuery("#viewboxOverlay").height(jQuery(document).height()); 
            jQuery(window).load(function() {
                jQuery("#viewboxOverlay").height(jQuery(document).height()); 
            });
            var thePostToPrintHasBeenClosed=false;
			jQuery("body").click(function(e) {
				onclickbody(e);
			});
			
			function onclickbody(e) {
								if(thePostToPrintHasBeenClosed){
										return;
				}
			
								var target = null;
				if (e != null){
					target = jQuery(e.target);
				}
								if (target == null || target.parents(".related-scoops").length===0 
						&amp;&amp; target.parents(".feedbackBannerContent").length===0 
						&amp;&amp; target.parents("#headbanner").length===0 
						&amp;&amp; target.parents("#moreInfoBlock").length === 0 
						&amp;&amp; target.parents("#thePostToPrint").length === 0 
						&amp;&amp; target.parents(".simplemodal-data").length === 0
						&amp;&amp; target.parents("#leadgen-container").length === 0
						&amp;&amp; !target.hasClass("simplemodal-overlay") 
						&amp;&amp; !target.hasClass("simplemodal-data") 
						&amp;&amp; !target.hasClass("simplemodal-close")) {
					closePostAndViewTopic(4038445557, "/t/technology-in-business-today", 1058404, "http://www.scoop.it/t/technology-in-business-today/p/4038445557/2015/03/04/top-smartphones-mobile-gadgets-from-mobile-world-congress-2015", '/t/technology-in-business-today',  null , 'false', 'Technology in Business Today | Scoop.it');
					thePostToPrintHasBeenClosed = true;
				}
			}
			jQuery("#thePostToPrint .htmlfragment").show();                
            
        });
      </script>

                    <div class="post-comment-container" id="comment_71715340">
                     <div class="post-comment">
                      <a class="preview-profile post-comment-avatar-link" href="/u/russell-r-roberts-jr">
                       <img class="post-comment-avatar" height="32px" src="http://img.scoop.it/lR6qgQ5Bi0xZKJZgFhb3ente7K7FKzbUk9Fz-4VREs0=" width="32px"/>

                      <div class="post-comment-content post-comment-insight ">
                       <a class="post-comment-author preview-profile" href="/u/russell-r-roberts-jr">
                        Russell R. Roberts, Jr.
                       </a>
                       <span>
                        's curator insight,
                       </span>
                       <span class="post-comment-date">
                        <a class="post-comment-date" href="/t/h-by-russell-r-roberts-jr/p/4047171755/2015/07/06/people-are-starting-to-call-apple-s-safari-web-browser-the-new-internet-explorer">
                         July 6, 9:15 PM
                        </a>
                       </span>
                       <div class="post-comment-text">
                        <span>
                         <p>
                          It's sad to see the current state of the Safari web browser. If developers aren't designing websites to use it, Safari may become outdated and end its days as a computer curiosity. I've tried Safari a few times--it isn't bad, but it surely isn't as as fast or flexible as Firefox, Chrome, or Opera. I gave up on Internet Explorer a long time ago. I prefer Chrome and Opera for my computer tasks. Your mileage may differ. Aloha, Russ.
                         </p>
                        </span>

                 <h2 class="h2 postTitleView">

                    <div class="post-comment-container" id="comment_71667688">
                     <div class="post-comment">
                      <a class="preview-profile post-comment-avatar-link" href="/u/russell-r-roberts-jr">
                       <img class="post-comment-avatar" height="32px" src="http://img.scoop.it/lR6qgQ5Bi0xZKJZgFhb3ente7K7FKzbUk9Fz-4VREs0=" width="32px"/>

                      <div class="post-comment-content post-comment-insight ">
                       <a class="post-comment-author preview-profile" href="/u/russell-r-roberts-jr">
                        Russell R. Roberts, Jr.
                       </a>
                       <span>
                        's curator insight,
                       </span>
                       <span class="post-comment-date">
                        <a class="post-comment-date" href="/t/h-by-russell-r-roberts-jr/p/4047110484/2015/07/05/wave-power-could-supply-half-the-u-s-with-cheap-electricity">
                         July 5, 11:18 PM
                        </a>
                       </span>
                       <div class="post-comment-text">
                        <span>
                         <p>
                          Intriguing essay on the use of wave power to generate electricity. Several nations, including France, are already using some of this technology to supply their energy needs. Even in the state of Hawaii, there is some investigation of this often ignored energy resource. The Natural Energy Laboratory Authority of Hawaii near Kailua-Kona has been looking into using various forms of wave power, including ocean thermal energy. This is another renewable energy source that should be supported. Aloha, Russ.
                         </p>
                        </span>

                    <a data-text="Tips on how to Use Social Media to Bolster your Brand" data-url="http://sco.lt/8oDxwH" data-via="scoopit" href="https://twitter.com/share">
                    </a>
                   </span>
                   <span class="share-button share-button-gp">
                    <div class="g-plusone" data-callback="googlePlusTouched" data-href="http://www.scoop.it/t/technology-in-business-today/p/4047139463/2015/07/06/tips-on-how-to-use-social-media-to-bolster-your-brand" data-size="medium">

                   <div class="commentList" id="4047139463_commentListContent">
                    <div class="post-comment-container" id="comment_71717269">
                     <div class="post-comment">
                      <a class="preview-profile post-comment-avatar-link" href="/u/russell-r-roberts-jr">
                       <img class="post-comment-avatar" height="32px" src="http://img.scoop.it/lR6qgQ5Bi0xZKJZgFhb3ente7K7FKzbUk9Fz-4VREs0=" width="32px"/>
                      </a>
                      <div class="post-comment-delete">
                      </div>
                      <div class="post-comment-content post-comment-insight ">
                       <a class="post-comment-author preview-profile" href="/u/russell-r-roberts-jr">
                        Russell R. Roberts, Jr.
                       </a>
                       <span>
                        's curator insight,
                       </span>
                       <span class="post-comment-date">
                        <a class="post-comment-date" href="/t/h-by-russell-r-roberts-jr/p/4047180180/2015/07/06/tips-on-how-to-use-social-media-to-bolster-your-brand">
                         July 6, 9:49 PM
                        </a>
                       </span>
                       <div class="post-comment-text">
                        <span>
                         <p>
                          Some excellent advice from
                          <a href="http://www.infusionsoft.com" rel="nofollow">
                           http://www.infusionsoft.com
                          </a>
                          . Social media can boost your brand if you do the following:
                         </p>
                         <p>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Start with the right platform. Use a social media platform that fits your business and your client base. Not everyone reads facebook.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Use consistent visuals across all of your social media and websites.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Use consistent voice and compatible content.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Be consistent in person. Don't fake it. Be yourself.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          What isn't working isn't helping. Avoid trendy fads. Serve your community and your customers.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Good luck!
                         </p>
                         <p>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Aloha, Russ.
                         </p>
                         <p>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                         </p>
                        </span>

                       <span class="post-comment-date">
                        <a class="post-comment-date" href="/t/h-by-russell-r-roberts-jr/p/4047112365/2015/07/05/record-breaking-flight-shows-the-power-of-solar-energy">
                         July 5, 11:12 PM

                       </span>
                       <div class="post-comment-text">
                        <span>
                         <p>
                          When the Solar Impulse 2 landed early Friday morning at Oahu's Kalaeloa Airport outside of Honolulu, it set more than just a record distance for solo flight. The solar-powered aircraft showed how well solar cells under extreme conditions could function in hostile environments. The around the world adventure of the Solar Impulse 2 serves as a test bed for advanced solar cell systems, battery technology, and revolutionary engine designs. Aloha, Russ.
                         </p>

window.twttr.ready(function (twttr) {

	});

function linkedinShareSuccess(e) {
	var location = jQuery(".linkedin-share-button[data-href='"+e+"']").attr("data-location");
	var url = e;
	trackNativeButtonShare('linkedin', location, url);
}




window.___gcfg = {
    parsetags: 'explicit'

(function() {
    var po = document.createElement('script'); po.type = 'text/javascript'; po.async = true;
    po.src = 'https://apis.google.com/js/plusone.js';
    var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; s.parentNode.insertBefore(po, s);
})();
  
  
function googlePlusTouched(e) {
	if (e.state == "on") {
		var url = e.href;
		var location = "bottomOfPost";
		trackNativeButtonShare('google', location, url);
	}
}


function loadSocialWidgetInAPost(post) {
	if (post.length &gt; 0) {
		//facebook
		if (typeof FB != 'undefined') {
			FB.XFBML.parse(jQuery(".share-button-fb",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-fb");
		}
		//twitter
		if (typeof twttr != 'undefined') {
			jQuery(".share-button-tw a", post).addClass("twitter-share-button");
			twttr.widgets.load(jQuery(".share-button-tw",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-tw");
		}
		//G+
		if (typeof gapi != 'undefined') {
			gapi.plusone.go(jQuery(".share-button-gp",post)[0]);
			post.addClass("loaded-gp");
		}
	}
}


function loadVisibleSharers() {
	jQuery(".post").each(function(){
		var elt = jQuery(this);
		if (elt.attr("id") == "topic-tags-widget") {
			return;
		}
		if (elt.hasClass("loaded-tw") &amp;&amp; elt.hasClass("loaded-gp") &amp;&amp; elt.hasClass("loaded-fb")) {return;}
		if (elt.isOnScreen()) {
			loadSocialWidgetInAPost(elt);
		}
	});
}

jQuery(window).bind("resize", function(event) {
	loadVisibleSharers();
});

var scrollingChecker = 0;
function onScroll(event) {
	clearTimeout(scrollingChecker);
	scrollingChecker = setTimeout(onStopScrolling, 300);
}

function onStopScrolling() {
	loadVisibleSharers();
}

jQuery(document).bind("scroll", onScroll);
